                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * The logic is as follows:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 1. Stream the document until a start marker is found.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 2. Switch to the app stream and stream it until an end marker is found. This is the non-suspended shell.\n'[39m +

                    [32m' * 5. Switch back to the document stream and stream the remainder (closing body and html tags).\n'[39m +

                    [32m' * @param outerHtml The stream for the document shell (`<Document>`).\n'[39m +
                    [32m" * @param innerHtml The stream for the application's content.\n"[39m +
                    [32m' * @param startMarker The marker in the document to start injecting the app.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * @param endMarker The marker in the app stream that signals the end of the initial, non-suspended render.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function splitStreamOnFirstNonHoistedTag(sourceStream) {\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                    const { done, value } = await sourceReader.read();\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                        const appPart = buffer.slice(match.index);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        buffer = "";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(hoistedPart));\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        controller.close();\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        hoistedTagsDone = true;\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                    controller.error(e);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    if (appBodyController) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                        appBodyController.error(e);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            };\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            pump().catch((e) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                controller.error(e);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                if (appBodyController) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    appBodyController.error(e);\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        },\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const appBodyStream = new ReadableStream({\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        start(controller) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            appBodyController = controller;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        },\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return [hoistedTagsStream, appBodyStream];\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\n'[39m +
                    [32m'/**\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * A utility that orchestrates and interleaves three ReadableStreams to produce a\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * single, valid HTML response stream. It uses two special markers:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * - `startMarker`: Placed in the `outerHtml` stream (the document shell) to\n'[39m +
                    [32m" *   designate where the application's content should be injected.\n"[39m +
                    [32m" * - `endMarker`: Injected into the `innerHtml` stream's RSC payload to signal\n"[39m +
                    [32m' *   the end of the initial, non-suspended render. This marker is needed for\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   non-blocking hydration, as it allows the stitching process to send the\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   client `<script>` tags before all suspended content has resolved.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * It manages three main stream readers:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * - `hoistedTagsReader`: Reads from the `hoistedTagsStream`, which contains only\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   the hoisted meta tags (e.g., `<title>`, `<meta>`).\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * - `outerReader`: Reads from the `outerHtml` stream, which is the server-rendered\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   document shell (containing `<html>`, `<head>`, etc.).\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * - `innerReader`: Reads from the `appBodyStream`, which contains the main\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *   application content, stripped of its hoisted tags.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * The function proceeds through a multi-phase state machine, managed by the\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * `pump` function, to correctly interleave these streams.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * The state machine moves through the following phases:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 1. `read-hoisted`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Goal:** Buffer all hoisted tags from the `hoistedTagsStream`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** Reads from `hoistedTagsReader` and appends all content into\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      the `hoistedTagsBuffer`. Does not enqueue anything yet.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Transition:** Moves to `outer-head` when the stream is exhausted.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 2. `outer-head`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Goal:** Stream the document up to the closing `</head>` tag, inject the\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      hoisted tags, and then continue until the app `startMarker`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** Reads from `outerReader`. When it finds `</head>`, it enqueues\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      the content before it, then enqueues the `hoistedTagsBuffer`, and finally\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      enqueues the `</head>` tag itself. It then continues reading from\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      `outerReader` until it finds the `startMarker`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Transition:** Moves to `inner-shell` after finding and discarding the\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      `startMarker`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 3. `inner-shell`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Goal:** Stream the initial, non-suspended part of the application.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** Switches to `innerReader`. It enqueues chunks until it finds\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      the `endMarker`. Any content after the marker is stored in\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      `innerSuspendedRemains`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Transition:** Moves to `outer-tail` after finding the `endMarker`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 4. `outer-tail`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m" *    - **Goal:** Stream the rest of the document's `<body>`, including client\n"[39m +
                    [32m' *      `<script>` tags.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** Switches back to `outerReader` and enqueues chunks until it\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      finds the `</body>` tag.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Transition:** Moves to `inner-suspended` after finding `</body>`.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 5. `inner-suspended`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Goal:** Stream any suspended content from the React app.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** First enqueues any content from `innerSuspendedRemains`, then\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      continues reading from `innerReader` until the stream is exhausted.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Transition:** Moves to `outer-end` when the stream is exhausted.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *\n'[39m +
                    [32m' * 6. `outer-end`:\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Goal:** Finish the document.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *    - **Action:** Switches back to `outerReader` for the last time to send the\n'[39m +
                    [32m' *      closing `</body>` and `</html>` tags.\n'[39m +
                    [32m' */\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function stitchDocumentAndAppStreams(outerHtml, innerHtml, startMarker, endMarker) {\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    let innerReader;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let hoistedTagsReader;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let buffer = "";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    let outerBufferRemains = "";\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    let hoistedTagsReady = false;\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    const pump = async (controller) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        const enqueue = (text) => {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            if (text) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(text));\n'[39m +

                    [32m'                // content. Once the stream is finished, transition to the next phase.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                const { done, value } = await hoistedTagsReader.read();\n'[39m +
                    [32m"                // When the stream is done, we're ready to process the document head.\n"[39m +
                    [32m'                if (done) {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    hoistedTagsReady = true;\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    phase = "outer-head";\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                else {\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    // Otherwise, keep appending to the buffer.\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                    hoistedTagsBuffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });\n'[39m +
                    [32m'                }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            }\n'[39m +
                    [32m'            else if (phase === "outer-h'[39m... 9656 more characters,
                  isTruncated: [33mfalse[39m

            [32m'- NEVER skip hooks (--no-verify, --no-gpg-sign, etc) unless the user explicitly requests it\n'[39m +

When a pre-commit hook fails, the commit did NOT happen  — so --amend would modify the PREVIOUS commit, which may result in destroying work or losing previous changes. Instead, after hook failure, fix the issue, re-stage, and create a NEW commit\n'[39m +
            [32m'- When staging files, prefer adding specific files by name rather than using "git add -A" or "git add .", which can accidentally include sensitive files (.env, credentials) or large binaries\n'[39m +
